16px;max-width: 100%;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;letter-spacing: 1px;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box !important;\">然而，安庆知府张文锦，不仅不肯开城门投降，反而带领着手底下的几千人站在城门上痛骂宁王。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 16px;margin-left: 16px;max-width: 100%;font-family: Optima-Regular, !important;\">生气的后果，双方开打。但安庆城易守难攻，而且张文锦在收到宁王军队沿长江而下的消息后就组织兵马、城中做足了准备。因此，宁王的部队几次进军，都没能更进一步。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 16px;margin-left: 16px;max-width: 100%;font-family: !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">兵贵精不贵多</strong></span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">”的原则，又是一番筛选，最后留下了包括正式官兵在内的两万多人。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 16px;margin-left: 16px;max-width: style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">“擒贼先擒王”与“临阵换将，兵家大忌”，说的也正是这个道理。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">”，朱宸濠认为很不吉利，把那人砍了。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 16px;margin-left: 16px;max-width: 100%;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;letter-spacing: 1px;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 16px;margin-left: 16px;max-width: 100%;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;letter-spacing: 1px;white-space: 38);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">一行人奔逃至此，本就惊魂未定，前面吃了两三次败仗，又见朱宸濠这样的举动，当下就有很多人计划着要逃。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 16px;margin-left: 16px;max-width: 100%;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;letter-spacing: 1px;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 16px;margin-left: 16px;max-width: 100%;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;letter-spacing: 1px;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">人心凉了，方寸乱了，队伍也就散了。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 16px;margin-left: 16px;max-width: 100%;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;letter-spacing: 1px;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 16px;margin-left: 16px;max-width: 100%;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;letter-spacing: 1px;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);text-align: !important;\">等宁王残部退到了樵舍安定下来，朱宸濠问计刘、李二人。刘分析说是王阳明那些船都是小船，很灵活，而己方都是大船，这就给了那些小船到处穿插捣乱的机会，所以应该把船用铁索锁在一起，不给那些小船可乘之机。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 16px;margin-left: 16px;max-width: 100%;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;letter-spacing: 1px;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 16px;margin-left: 16px;max-width: 100%;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;letter-spacing: 1px;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">铁索连船的事，《三国演义》赤壁之战有记载，曹军被火烧了赤壁；就明朝，陈友谅在鄱阳湖上叫板洪武帝朱元璋也是用的这个法子，结果火烧鄱阳湖。即便有前车之鉴，朱宸濠还是赞同了刘养正的看法。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 16px;margin-left: 16px;max-width: 100%;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;letter-spacing: 1px;text-align: center;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: !important;\">宁王的船目标过于明显，因此，朱宸濠告知渔民身份，要求搭渔船登岸，说是金银珠宝都给这些渔民。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 16px;margin-left: 16px;max-width: 100%;font-family: Optima-Regular, 16px;max-width: 100%;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;letter-spacing: 1px;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box !important;\">大明最后一位宁王朱宸濠，从起义到被擒，前后不过四十多天。而王阳明自讨伐叛逆，到鄱阳湖决战全歼叛军，总共不过十天，这正是“</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">以万余乌合之兵，而破强寇十万之众</strong></span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">”。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 16px;margin-left: 16px;max-width: 100%;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;letter-spacing: 1px;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"></span><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"></section><section style=\"margin-right: 16px;margin-left: 16px;max-width: 100%;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;letter-spacing: 1px;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">《明史》载，“宸濠喜，时时诇中朝事，闻谤言辄喜。或言帝明圣，朝廷治，即怒”。后世人常以此作为朱宸濠庸碌之辈的论断，深不以为然。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 16px;margin-left: 16px;max-width: 100%;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;letter-spacing: 1px;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 16px;margin-left: 16px;max-width: 100%;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;letter-spacing: 1px;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">朱宸濠十年谋划，这需要相当的隐忍；发难时先灭孙燧，后追杀王阳明，知谁能为己用而谁又不能为己所用，说明有一定的识人眼力；散布武宗是民间野种，而非大明血脉，知道造舆论与用钱上下打点，又有一定的手段。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 16px;margin-left: 16px;max-width: 100%;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;letter-spacing: 1px;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 16px;margin-left: 16px;max-width: 100%;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;letter-spacing: 1px;white-space: 38);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">然而他的对手是千古一人的王阳明，王阳明不带兵冲锋陷阵，这是武将的路数。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 16px;margin-left: 16px;max-width: 100%;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;letter-spacing: 1px;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">他玩的是脑子，能够</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word
